    function setCookie(name, value) {
        document.cookie = name + "=" + value;
    }
    function getCookie(name) {
        var r = document.cookie.match("(^|;) ?" + name + "=([^;]*)(;|$)");
        if (r) return r[2];
        else return "";
    }
    function deleteCookie(name) {
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() - 1);
        document.cookie = name += "=; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
    }
    ////
    function getParameterByName() {
        var vars = [], hash;
        var hashes = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');
        for(var i = 0; i < hashes.length; i++)
        {
            hash = hashes[i].split('=');
            vars.push(hash[0]);
            vars[hash[0]] = hash[1];
        }
        return vars;
    }
            var source = 'Direct';
    var medium = 'direct';
    var campaign = '';
    var keyword = '';


    // Set the cookies
    if(source != '' && ( getCookie('utm_source') == null || getCookie('utm_source') == "" || getCookie('utm_source') == "undefined")) {
        setCookie('utm_source', source);
    }
    if(medium != '' && (getCookie('utm_medium') == null || getCookie('utm_medium') == "" || getCookie('utm_medium') == "undefined")) {
        setCookie('utm_medium', medium);
    }
    if(campaign != '' && (getCookie('utm_campaign') == null || getCookie('utm_campaign') == "" || getCookie('utm_campaign') == "undefined")) {
        setCookie('utm_campaign', campaign);
    }
    if(keyword != '' && (getCookie('utm_keyword') == null || getCookie('utm_keyword') == "" || getCookie('utm_keyword') == "undefined")) {
        setCookie('utm_keyword', keyword);
    }

<span class="descr">
* Prețul dispozitivului este prezentat orientativ. Valoarea exactă a produsului o puteți afla la consultanții Darwin. Dacă dispuneți de încărcătorul, cablul USB și cutia originală, iar dispozitivul nu prezintă zgîrîieturi semnificative, deformări, ecran spart sau lipsa pieselor interioare, prețul acestuia poate atinge valoarea cea mai apropiată celei prezentate mai sus! </span>
</div>
<script type="dba6ac1e5f7eb31e24999cfe-text/javascript">
    const isProduct = 'true';
    var isFirstChange = false;
    function getCategory(input_no){
        var select = $('select[name="category"]')[input_no];
        var option = $(select).find('option:selected');
        var regionid = option.attr('value');
        var brands = $('select[name="brand"]')[input_no];
        $(brands).find('option').each(function() {
            if($( this ).attr('data-category') == regionid){
                $( this ).addClass('rblock');
                $( this ).removeAttr('disabled');
            } else {
                $( this ).removeClass('rblock');
            }
        });
        $(brands).find('option.rblock:first').prop('selected', true).trigger('change');
    }
    function getBrand(input_no){
        var select = $('select[name="brand"]')[input_no];
        var option = $(select).find('option:selected');
        var regionid = option.attr('value');

        var select2 = $('select[name="category"]')[input_no];
        var option2 = $(select2).find('option:selected');
        var regionid2 = option2.attr('value');

        var models = $('select[name="model"]')[input_no];

        $(models).find('option').each(function( index ) {
            if($( this ).val() != '') {
                if($( this ).attr('data-brand') == regionid && $( this ).attr('data-category') == regionid2){
                    $( this ).addClass('rblock');
                    $( this ).removeAttr('disabled');
                } else {
                    $( this ).removeClass('rblock');
                    $( this ).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                }
            }
        });
        $(models).find('option.rblock:first').prop('selected', true).trigger('change');
        if(option.val() == '') {
            $('.price-container'+input_no).addClass('d-none');
        } else {
            $('.price-container'+input_no).removeClass('d-none');
        }
    }
    function getProdus(input_no){
        var select = $('select[name="model"]')[input_no];
        var option = $(select).find('option:selected');
        var price = option.attr('data-price');
        var image = option.attr('data-image');
        $(select).closest('.select-trade-in').find('.image-ajax').attr('src', image);
        setPrices();
    }
    function setPrices() {
        var getDifference,
            getPriceNew1 = $('#model_0 option:selected').attr('data-price'),
            getPriceNew2 = $('#model_1 option:selected').attr('data-price'),
            priceForOld = 0;
        if(getPriceNew1 != undefined && getPriceNew2 != undefined){
            priceForOld = Math.round(parseFloat(getPriceNew2) * 0.75);
        }
        if(priceForOld > parseFloat(getPriceNew1) && getPriceNew1 != undefined && getPriceNew2 != undefined) {
            priceForOld = getPriceNew1;
            getDifference = parseFloat(getPriceNew2) - parseInt(getPriceNew1);
        } else if(priceForOld < parseFloat(getPriceNew1) && getPriceNew1 != undefined && getPriceNew2 != undefined) {
            getDifference = parseFloat(getPriceNew2) - priceForOld;
            if(isProduct != 'true' || isFirstChange == true) {
                toastr.warning("Suma oferită poate constitui maxim 75% din prețul produsului nou ales");
            }
        }
        else{
            priceForOld = getPriceNew1;
            getDifference = getPriceNew2;
        }
        $('.price-ajax-0').text(priceForOld);
        $('.price-ajax-1').text(getDifference);
    }
    setTimeout(function(){
        if(isProduct == 'true') {
            $('#brand_1').find("option[data-is-selected='true']").prop('selected', true).trigger('change');
            $('option[data-is-selected="true"]').attr('selected', true);
            $('.product img').attr('src', $('.product').closest('[name="brand"]').find('[data-is-selected="true"]').data('image'));
            $('.select-trade-in').each(function () {
                var $that = $(this),
                    selected_product = $that.find('select[name="model"]').find('[data-is-selected="true"]').prop('selected', true),
                    image = selected_product.data('image');

                $that.find('[name="category"]').trigger('change');
                $that.find('[name="brand"]').find('[data-is-selected="true"]').prop('selected', true).trigger('change');
                $that.find('[name="model"]').find('[data-is-selected="true"]').prop('selected', true).trigger('change');
                $that.find('.image-ajax').attr('src', image);
            });
        }
    }, 0);
    $('select[name="category"]').change(function(input){
        var getSelected = input.currentTarget;
        var getId = $(getSelected).attr('id');
        var getNumber = parseInt(getId.split('_')[1]);
        getCategory(getNumber);
    });
    $('select[name="brand"]').change(function(input){
        var getSelected = input.currentTarget;
        var getId = $(getSelected).attr('id');
        var getNumber = parseInt(getId.split('_')[1]);
        getBrand(getNumber);
    });
    $('select[name="model"]').change(function(input){
        var getSelected = input.currentTarget;
        var getId = $(getSelected).attr('id');
        var getNumber = parseInt(getId.split('_')[1]);
        getProdus(getNumber);
    });
    $(document).ready(function(){
        isFirstChange = true;
    });
</script> <div class="vertical-hr"></div>

    var city = "city_ro";
    var address = "address_ro";
    var grafic = "grafic_ro";

    $(window).on("load", function () {
        var d = true;
        if ($(window).width() < 768) {
            d = false;
        }
        $map1 = L.map('map-trade-in', {dragging: d, attributionControl: false}).setView([47.0045067, 28.8413991], 7);
        $map1.zoomControl.setPosition('bottomright');
        $map1.scrollWheelZoom.disable();

        L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png').addTo($map1);

        var dico = L.Icon.extend({
            options: {
                iconUrl: 'https://darwin.md/img/marker_darwin.png',
                iconSize: [41, 64],
                iconAnchor: [20, 64],
                popupAnchor: [1, -60]
            }
        });

        var darwinIcon = new dico();

        jQuery.each(shops, function (c, cityShops) {
            cityShops.forEach(function (e, i) {
                var location = e["location"].split(",");
                popupContent = '' +
                    '<div style="width:270px">'
                    + '<img src="https://darwin.md/img/logo_black.png" alt="Darwin">   '
                    + '<p><span style="font-size:16px;">' + e[city] + ' ' + e[address] + '</span>'
                    + '<br><span style="font-size:12px;">' + e[grafic] + '</span><br>'
                    + '</p>'
                    + '<div class="map-marker-info">'
                    + '<span style="font-size:14px;">'
                    + '<a class="mr-3" href="tel:' + e["phone"] + '">' + e["phone"] + '</a>'
                    + '<a class="mr-3" href="mailto:' + e["email"] + '">' + e["email"] + '</a>'
                    + '</span>'
                    + '<p class="d-none map-marker-bottom" data-shop-id="' + e["shop_id"] + '">';
                        if(e.panorama) {
                            popupContent = popupContent + '<a href="/shop/' + e['shop_id'] + '" class="galley_360"><i class="icon-icon_360"></i></a>';
                        }
                        popupContent = popupContent + '<a class="gallery_shop"><i class="icon-icon_obiective"></i></a>'
                    + '</p>'
                    + '</div>'
                    + '</div>';
                $shop_marker1 = L.marker([location[0], location[1]], {icon: darwinIcon}).addTo($map1);
                $shop_marker1.bindPopup(popupContent);
            });
        });
    });

    function updateMap1(c, key, el) {
        // Add active class to li element
        $(el).closest('.map_ctx').find('a:not(".capital-show-locations")').removeClass('active');
        $(el).addClass('active');
        // Get store by index position
        var store = shops[c][key];
        var location = store["location"].split(",");
        popupContent = '' +
            '<div style="width:270px">'
            + '<img class="img-fluid" src="https://darwin.md/img/logo_black.png" alt="Darwin">'
            + '<p><span style="font-size:16px;">' + store[city] + ' ' + store[address] + '</span>'
            + '<br><span style="font-size:12px;">' + store[grafic] + '</span><br>'
            + '</p>'
            + '<div class="map-marker-info">'
            + '<span style="font-size:14px;">'
            + '<a class="mr-3" href="tel:' + store["phone"] + '">' + store["phone"] + '</a>'
            + '<a class="mr-3" href="mailto:' + store["email"] + '">' + store["email"] + '</a>'
            + '</span>'
            + '<p class="d-none map-marker-bottom" data-shop-id="' + store["shop_id"] + '">';
                if(store.panorama) {
                    popupContent = popupContent + '<a href="/shop/' + store['shop_id'] + '" class="galley_360"><i class="icon-icon_360"></i></a>';
                }
                popupContent = popupContent + '<a class="gallery_shop"><i class="icon-icon_obiective"></i></a>'
            + '</p>'
            + '</div>'
            + '</div>';
        // Update map
        $shop_marker1.setLatLng([location[0], location[1]]).update();
        $shop_marker1.bindPopup(popupContent).openPopup();
        $map1.setView([location[0], location[1]], 14);
        $map1.flyTo([location[0], location[1]]);
    }
</script> </div>
</div>

        $map.scrollWheelZoom.disable();

        L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png').addTo($map);

        var dico = L.Icon.extend({
            options: {
                iconUrl: 'https://darwin.md/img/marker_darwin.png',
                iconSize: [41, 64],
                iconAnchor: [20, 64],
                popupAnchor: [1, -60]
            }
        });

        var darwinIcon = new dico();

        jQuery.each(shops, function (c, cityShops) {
            cityShops.forEach(function (e, i) {
                var location = e["location"].split(",");
                popupContent = '' +
                    '<div style="width:270px">'
                    + '<img src="https://darwin.md/img/logo_black.png" alt="Darwin">   '
                    + '<p><span style="font-size:16px;">' + e[city] + ' ' + e[address] + '</span>'
                    + '<br><span style="font-size:12px;">' + e[grafic] + '</span><br>'
                    + '</p>'
                    + '<div class="map-marker-info">'
                    + '<span style="font-size:14px;">'
                    + '<a class="mr-3" href="tel:' + e["phone"] + '">' + e["phone"] + '</a>'
                    + '<a class="mr-3" href="mailto:' + e["email"] + '">' + e["email"] + '</a>'
                    + '</span>'
                    + '<p class="map-marker-bottom" data-shop-id="' + e["shop_id"] + '">';
                        if(e.panorama) {
                            popupContent = popupContent + '<a href="/shop/' + e['shop_id'] + '" class="galley_360"><i class="icon-icon_360"></i></a>';
                        }
                        if(e.img1 && e.img1 != 'images/no-photo.png'){
                            popupContent = popupContent + '<a class="gallery_shop"><i class="icon-icon_obiective"></i></a>'
                        }
                    + '</p>'
                    + '</div>'
                    + '</div>';
                $shop_marker = L.marker([location[0], location[1]], {icon: darwinIcon}).addTo($map);
                $shop_marker.bindPopup(popupContent);
            });
        });

        $('.sort-by-location').click(function () {
                $map.locate();
                $map.on('locationfound', function (data) {
                    L.marker([data.latitude, data.longitude]).addTo($map);
                    L.circle([data.latitude, data.longitude], data.accuracy, {
                        weight: 1,
                        color: '#267fca',
                        setOpacity: 0.1
                    }).addTo($map);
                    orderStores(data.latlng, 'pick-up-map');
                    user_located = true;
                });
        });
    });

    function updateMap(c, key, el) {
        // Add active class to li element
        $(el).closest('.map_ctx').find('a:not(".capital-show-locations")').removeClass('active');
        $(el).addClass('active');
        // Get store by index position
        var store = shops[c][key];
        var location = store["location"].split(",");
        popupContent = '' +
            '<div style="width:270px">'
            + '<img class="img-fluid" src="https://darwin.md/img/logo_black.png" alt="Darwin">'
            + '<p><span style="font-size:16px;">' + store[city] + ' ' + store[address] + '</span>'
            + '<br><span style="font-size:12px;">' + store[grafic] + '</span><br>'
            + '</p>'
            + '<div class="map-marker-info">'
            + '<span style="font-size:14px;">'
            + '<a class="mr-3" href="tel:' + store["phone"] + '">' + store["phone"] + '</a>'
            + '<a class="mr-3" href="mailto:' + store["email"] + '">' + store["email"] + '</a>'
            + '</span>'
            + '<p class="map-marker-bottom" data-shop-id="' + store["shop_id"] + '">';
                if(store.panorama) {
                    popupContent = popupContent + '<a href="/shop/' + store['shop_id'] + '" class="galley_360"><i class="icon-icon_360"></i></a>';
                }
                if(store.img1 && store.img1 != 'images/no-photo.png'){
                    popupContent = popupContent + '<a class="gallery_shop"><i class="icon-icon_obiective"></i></a>'
                }
            + '</p>'
            + '</div>'
            + '</div>';
        // Update map
        $shop_marker.setLatLng([location[0], location[1]]).update();
        $shop_marker.bindPopup(popupContent).openPopup();
        $map.setView([location[0], location[1]], 14);
        $map.flyTo([location[0], location[1]]);
    }
    function orderStores(user_location, id_map) {
        var $parent = $('#'+id_map).closest('.map_ctx');
        var $stores = $parent.find($('.cities .htag'));
        var $store = $parent.find($('.cities .htag a'));
        var $locations = $stores.children('a:not(.capital-show-locations, .city-zone, .capital-north-show-locations)');

        $locations.sort(function (a, b) {
            var a_location = {lat: $(a).data('lat'), lng: $(a).data('lng')};
            var b_location = {lat: $(b).data('lat'), lng: $(b).data('lng')};
            var a_distance = haversineDistance(user_location, a_location);
            var b_distance = haversineDistance(user_location, b_location);
            if (a_distance > b_distance) {
                return 1;
            }
            if (a_distance < b_distance) {
                return -1;
            }
            return 0;
        });

        $store.removeClass('selected');
        if ($($locations[0]).data('category') == "capital"){
            $stores.find($('.capital-show-locations')).trigger('click');
            $stores.find($('.city-zone[data-zone="'+$($locations[0]).data('zone')+'"]')).trigger('click');
        }
        if ($($locations[0]).data('category') == "north-capital"){
           $stores.find($('.capital-north-show-locations')).trigger('click');
        }

        $locations.detach().appendTo($stores);
        $map.setView([$($locations[0]).data('lat'), $($locations[0]).data('lng')], 13);

        $($locations[0]).trigger('click');
    }
    function haversineDistance(c1 = {}, c2 = {}) {
        var p = 0.017453292519943295;
        var c = Math.cos;
        var a = 0.5 - c((c2.lat - c1.lat) * p) / 2 + c(c1.lat * p) * c(c2.lat * p) * (1 - c((c2.lng - c1.lng) * p)) / 2;
        return 12742 * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(a));
    }
    $('body').on('click', '.map-marker-bottom a.gallery_shop',function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var shop_id = $(this).parent().data('shop-id');
        var gallery_popup = $('.shop-gallery-popup');
        $.ajax({
            url: '/shop_gallery',
            method: 'GET',
            data: {
                shop_id: shop_id
            },
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (response) {
                var gallery = [];
                for(var i = 0; i < response.shop_images.length; i++) {
                    gallery.push(
                        {
                            src  : response.shop_images[i],
                            type: 'image',
                            animationEffect: 'fade',
                            opts : {
                                thumb   : response.shop_images[i]
                            }
                        }
                    )
                }
                $.fancybox.open(gallery, {
                    loop : false
                });
            }
        })
    });
</script>

<script type="dba6ac1e5f7eb31e24999cfe-text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
        $('#area-emoji').emojioneArea({
            pickerPosition: "bottom",
            tonesStyle: "bullet",
        });
        $('#stars li').on('mouseover', function(){
            var onStar = parseInt($(this).data('value'), 10);
            $(this).parent().children('li.star').each(function(e){
                if (e < onStar) {
                    $(this).addClass('hover');
                } else {
                    $(this).removeClass('hover');
                }
            });
        }).on('mouseout', function(){
            $(this).parent().children('li.star').each(function(e){
                $(this).removeClass('hover');
            });
        });
        $('#stars li').on('click', function(){
            var onStar = parseInt($(this).data('value'), 10);
            var stars = $(this).parent().children('li.star');
            var ratingValue = parseInt($('#stars li.selected').last().data('value'), 10);
            var msg = "";
            for (i = 0; i < stars.length; i++) {
                $(stars[i]).removeClass('selected');
            }
            for (i = 0; i < onStar; i++) {
                $(stars[i]).addClass('selected');
            }
            msg = "Thanks!";
            //thanks(msg);

        });
    });
    $('#d_filephoto').change(function () {
        if(this.files.length){
            $('form .file-text').text(this.files[0].name);
        }
    });

    $(document).on("click", "button.save-comment", function (e) {

        var my_form = $('#modalComment');

        var idd = parseInt($('.p_id').text());
        var parent_id = parseInt(my_form.find('.d_parent_id').val());
        var star = parseInt($('#stars li.selected').last().data('value'));
        var name = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var phone_email = my_form.find('.d_phone_email').val();
        var body = my_form.find('.d_body').val();

        if (idd && body) {

            $('button.save-comment').attr("disabled", true);
            var form_data = new FormData();
                        var filephoto = $('#d_filephoto').prop('files')[0];
            form_data.append('photo', filephoto);
            form_data.append('name', name.trim());
            form_data.append('phone_email', phone_email.trim());
                        form_data.append('body', body.trim());
            form_data.append('idd', idd);
            form_data.append('parent_id', parent_id);
            form_data.append('star', star);
            form_data.append('type', 'product');
            $('button.save-comment').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

            $.ajax({
                url: '/' + lang + '/addComment',
                dataType: 'text',
                cache: false,
                contentType: false,
                processData: false,
                data: form_data,
                type: 'post',
                success: function (data) {
                    var data = JSON.parse(data);
                    if (data.success == 'ok') {
                        thanks(data.message, 1);
                        thanksMobile(data.message, 1, my_form);
                        $('button.save-comment').text(data.message);
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone_email, .d_body').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    } else {
                        thanks(data.message , 2);
                        thanksMobile(data.message, 2, my_form);
                    }
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $(my_form).find(".close").click();
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone_email, .d_body, .parent_id').val('');
                        $('button.save-comment').attr('disabled', false).text('Continua');
                    }, 2000);
                },
                error: function (resp) {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone_email, .d_body').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    if (resp.status == 406) {
                        var data1 = resp.responseText;
                        data2 = JSON.parse(data1);
                        data = data2.data;
                        $('button.save-comment').attr('disabled', false);
                        for (var item in data){
                            $(my_form).find(".d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                            thanks(data[item], 2);
                            thanksMobile(data[item], 2, my_form);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });

        } else {
                            if ((!parent_id) && isNaN(star) || star == "" || star == undefined || parseInt(star) <= 0){
                    thanks("Evalueaza cu o nota!", 2);
                    thanksMobile("Evalueaza cu o nota!", 2, my_form);
                } else {
                    thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
                    thanksMobile(complete_all_input, 2, my_form);
                }
                                                    if (name == "" || name == undefined){
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                } else {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                }
                if (phone_email == "" || phone_email == undefined){
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_phone_email').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                } else {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_phone_email').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                }
                        if (body == "" || body == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('.d_body').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('.d_body').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
            }
        }
        return true;
    });
</script>

        $(document).ready(function($) {

          let currentPage = "https://darwin.md/apple-iphone-12-pro-max-128-gb-blue.html";
          setTimeout(function (){
              $(window.BX.SiteButton.hello.config.conditions).map((i,v) => {
                  setTimeout(function () {
                      let textCurrentPage = v.pages.LIST[0];
                      currentPage == textCurrentPage ? $('#chatB24').text(v.text) : '';
                  },`${v.delay}000`)
              });
          },1000);

            var DoingTime = 0;
            // cosul pentru animatie a butonului de call  darwin
            bounce_button();
            function aut_of_block(){
                var period = 0;
                period++;
                if (period <=2) {
                    //show tooltip here
                    $('.tooltip_cont').css({'display': 'block'});
                    $('.tooltip_cont').animate({'opacity': 1}, 600);
                    /*setTimeout(function(){
                        $('.tooltip_cont').animate({
                            'opacity': 0},
                            500, function() {
                            $('.tooltip_cont').css({'display': 'none'});
                        });
                        bounce_button();
                    }, 5000);*/
                    DoingTime++;
                } else {
                    bounce_button();
                }
            }
            function bounce_button(){
                if (DoingTime < 2) {
                    var Execution = 0;
                    var DoAnim = setInterval(function(){
                            Execution++;
                        if (Execution <= 2) {
                            $('.apel').removeClass('active_roll_call');
                            $('.apel').addClass('bounce_button_active');
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                $('.apel').removeClass('bounce_button_active');
                                $('.apel').addClass('active_roll_call');
                            }, 600);
                        } else{
                            aut_of_block();
                            clearInterval(DoAnim);
                        }
                    }, 2000);
                } else {
                    var DoAnim = setInterval(function(){
                            $('.apel').removeClass('active_roll_call');
                            $('.apel').addClass('bounce_button_active');
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                $('.apel').removeClass('bounce_button_active');
                                $('.apel').addClass('active_roll_call');
                            }, 1200);
                    }, 4000);
                }
            }
        });
    </script>

<script type="dba6ac1e5f7eb31e24999cfe-text/javascript" charset="utf-8" async defer>
        function ajaxCredit() {
            var my_form = $('#tab-credit');

            var type = '0';if(type <= 0 || isNaN(type)){type = 1;}

            var price = '24999';
            var service1 = my_form.find('input[name="service1"]').is(':checked');
            var service2 = my_form.find('input[name="service2"]').is(':checked');
            var service3 = my_form.find('input[name="service3"]').is(':checked');
            var quantity = my_form.find('.quantity2 .amount').text().trim();
            if (type && price) {
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/' + lang + '/changeAllowedCredit',
                    type: 'POST',
                    data: {
                        type: type,
                        price: price,
                        service1: service1,
                        service2: service2,
                        service3: service3,
                        quantity: quantity
                    },
                    dataType: 'json',
                    success: function (data) {
                        if (data.success == 'ok') {
                            $('.credit-period').find('.cred1t').each(function () {
                                var mounth = $(this).data('period');
                                var price_mth = $(this).find('.h4 b');
                                price_mth.html(data.info[mounth].summa);
                                $(this).attr('data-percent', data.info[mounth].procent);

                                if($(this).hasClass('selected_credit')){
                                    $('.bubble .swiper-slide').removeClass('active_percent');
                                    $('.credit_ajax').html(data.info[mounth].creditmax);
                                    $('.service_ajax').html(data.info[mounth].service);
                                    $('.bonus_ajax').html(data.info[mounth].bonus);
                                    $('.total_ajax').html(data.info[mounth].summa);
                                    var tmp_percent = data.info[mounth].procent;
                                    var percent = 1;
                                    if(tmp_percent == 0){
                                        percent = 2;
                                    }else if(tmp_percent == 2){
                                        percent = 0;
                                    }
                                    $('.index_'+percent).addClass('active_percent');
                                    if (bubble != undefined) {
                                        bubble.slideTo( percent ,500,false );
                                    }
                                }
                            });
                        } else {
                            // thanks(data.message , 2);
                        }
                    }
                });
            } else {
                thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
            }
            // return false;
        }
        $(document).on("click", ".credit_up", function (e) {
            ajaxCredit();
        });
        $(document).on("change", ".credit_checks", function (e) {
            ajaxCredit();
        });

        var bubble = undefined;
        var mounthswiper = undefined;
        function sl_bubble() {
            if (window.innerWidth > 991 && $('.bubble').length) {
                if (bubble != undefined) {
                    bubble.update()
                } else {
                    bubble = new Swiper(".bubble", {
                        centeredSlides: true,
                        centeredSlidesBounds: true,
                        slidesPerView: 1,
                        watchOverflow: true,
                        watchSlidesVisibility: true,
                        watchSlidesProgress: true,
                        direction: 'vertical',
                    });
                }
            } else if ($('.bubble').length && window.innerWidth < 992 && bubble !== undefined) {
                bubble.destroy();
                bubble = undefined;
            }
        }
        function sl_mounthswiper() {
            if (window.innerWidth < 767 && $('.mounthswiper').length) {
                if (mounthswiper != undefined) {
                    mounthswiper.update()
                } else {
                    mounthswiper = new Swiper(".mounthswiper", {
                        grabCursor: true,
                        centeredSlides: true,
                        slidesPerView: 'auto',
                        spaceBetween: 16,
                        breakpoints: {
                            567: {
                                spaceBetween: 8,
                            },
                        },
                    });
                }
            } else if ($('.mounthswiper').length && window.innerWidth > 767 && mounthswiper !== undefined) {
                mounthswiper.destroy();
                mounthswiper = undefined;
            }
        }
        sl_bubble();
        sl_mounthswiper();
        $(window).on('load', ajaxCredit);
        $(window).on('resize', sl_mounthswiper);
        $(window).on('resize', sl_bubble);
        $('.box-check input').change(function() {
            $(".box-check input").parent().removeClass("selected-service");
            $(".box-check input:checked").parent().addClass("selected-service");
        });

            $('.cred1t').removeClass('selected_credit');
            $(this).addClass('selected_credit');

            var qty_text = $('.quantity2 .amount');

                $('.get_credit').removeAttr('disabled');
                $('.get_credit').css('opacity','1');
            } else {
                $('.get_credit').attr("disabled", "disabled");

        $(document).on("click", ".get_credit", function (e) {
            var my_form = $('#tab-credit');
            var name = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
            var phone = my_form.find('.d_phone').val();
            var product_name = $('.title h1').text();
            var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
            var price = '24 999';
            var quantity = my_form.find('.quantity2 .amount').text().trim();
            var percent = my_form.find('.active_percent ').text().trim();
            var type_credit = my_form.find('.selected_credit').text().trim();
                type_credit = type_credit + ' ' + percent + '; Cantitate:' +quantity;

            var service1 = my_form.find('input[name="service1"]').is(':checked');
            var service2 = my_form.find('input[name="service2"]').is(':checked');
            var service3 = my_form.find('input[name="service3"]').is(':checked');
            if(service1 == 1){
                type_credit = type_credit + ' +Furt;';
            }
            if(service2 == 1){
                type_credit = type_credit + ' +Extra;';
            }
            if(service3 == 1){
                type_credit = type_credit + ' +Extinsa;';
            }
            product_name = product_name.trim() + '; Credit:' + type_credit.trim();

            var web = 'https://darwin.md/apple-iphone-12-pro-max-128-gb-blue.html';
            if (name && phone) {
                $('button.get_credit').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/' + lang + '/getDetailsA',
                    type: 'POST',
                    data: {
                        name: name.trim(),
                        phone: phone.trim(),
                        product_name: product_name.trim(),
                        product_id: product_id.trim(),
                        price: price,
                        type_credit: type_credit.trim(),
                        web: web,
                        canal: 'credit'
                    },
                    dataType: 'json',
                    success: function (data) {
                        if (data.success == 'ok') {
                            thanks(data.message, 1);
                            $('button.get_credit').text(data.message);
                            $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                            window.location.hash = '#success-credit';
                            dataLayer.push({'event': 'comanda_credit_form'});
                            $( '<iframe src="https://creativecdn.com/tags?id=pr_9qCjFrtDD4j4umSzcbkn_orderstatus2_'+'24999'+'_'+data.order_id+'-loan_ro-'+product_id.trim()+'&cd=default&id=pr_9qCjFrtDD4j4umSzcbkn_custom_lang_ro" width="1" height="1"scrolling="no" frameBorder="0" style="display: none;"></iframe>' ).insertAfter( "footer" );
                                                            //sendDataLayerSuccessProduct(data.order_id);
                                                    } else {
                            thanks(data.message , 2);
                            thanksMobile(data.message , 2, $('#tab-credit'));
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (resp) {
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                        if (resp.status == 406) {
                            var data = resp.responseJSON.data;
                            $('button.get_credit').attr('disabled', false);
                            for (var item in data){
                                $(my_form).find("input.d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                                thanks(data[item], 2);
                                thanksMobile(data[item] , 2, $('#tab-credit'));
                            }
                            if(data === undefined || data.length == 0){
                                thanks(resp.responseJSON.message, 2);
                                thanksMobile(resp.responseJSON.message , 2, $('#tab-credit'));
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            } else {
                if (name == "" || name == undefined){
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
                } else {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
                }
                if (phone == "" || phone == undefined){
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
                } else {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
                }
                thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
                thanksMobile(complete_all_input , 2, $('#tab-credit'));
            }
            return true;
        });
    </script>

	$(document).on('click','#nl-terms', function (e) {
        if ($(this).find('input:checkbox:checked').length == 1){
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').removeAttr('disabled');
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').css('opacity','1');
        } else {
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').attr("disabled", "disabled");
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').css('opacity','0.5');
        }
    });
    $(document).on("click", ".subscribe_newsletter", function (element) {
        element.preventDefault();
        var form = $(element.target).closest('form');
        var validate = validateErrors(form);
        if(! validate) {
            return false;
        }
        $(element.target).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
        $.ajax({
            url: '/' + lang + '/newsletter/send',
            type: 'POST',
            data: form.serialize(),
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (data) {
                thanks(data.message , 2);
                form.trigger("reset").find('input').css("border", "");
                $(element.target).attr('disabled', false);
            },
            error: function (resp) {
                $(element.target).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                if (resp.success == false) {
                    validateJson(form, resp.responseJSON.data);
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="dba6ac1e5f7eb31e24999cfe-text/javascript">
    $(document).on("click", ".get_preorder", function (e) {

        var my_form = $('#preorder-form-modal');

        var name = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var phone = my_form.find('.d_phone').val();
        var product_name = $('.title h1').text();
        var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
        var price = '24 999';
        var web = 'https://darwin.md/apple-iphone-12-pro-max-128-gb-blue.html';
        var canal = 'preorder';
        var coming = '0';
        if(coming > 0){
            canal = 'coming';
        }

        if (name && phone) {
            $('button.get_preorder').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            $.ajax({
                url: '/' + lang + '/getDetailsA',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    name: name.trim(),
                    phone: phone.trim(),
                    product_name: product_name.trim(),
                    product_id: product_id.trim(),
                    price: price,
                    web: web,
                    canal: canal
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function (data) {
                    if (data.success == 'ok') {
                        thanks(data.message, 1);
                        my_form.find('.modal-body').empty().html('<h2>' + data.message + '</h2>');
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                        window.location.hash = '#success-more_details';
                                                    //sendDataLayerSuccessProduct(data.order_id);
                                            } else {
                        thanks(data.message , 2);
                        thanksMobile(data.message , 2, $('#preorder-form-modal'));
                    }
                },
                error: function (resp) {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    if (resp.status == 406) {
                        var data = resp.responseJSON.data;
                        $('button.get_preorder').attr('disabled', false);
                        for (var item in data){
                            $(my_form).find("input.d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                            thanks(data[item], 2);
                            thanksMobile(data[item] , 2, $('#preorder-form-modal'));
                        }
                        if(data === undefined || data.length == 0){
                            thanks(resp.responseJSON.message, 2);
                            thanksMobile(resp.responseJSON.message , 2, $('#preorder-form-modal'));
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } else {
            if (name == "" || name == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            if (phone == "" || phone == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
            thanksMobile(complete_all_input , 2, $('#preorder-form-modal'));
        }
        return true;
    });

    $(document).one("click", ".add_fav", function (e) {
        var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
        if(!$(this).hasClass('active')){
            $( '<iframe src="https://creativecdn.com/tags?id=pr_9qCjFrtDD4j4umSzcbkn_wishlist_ro-'+product_id.trim()+'&id=pr_9qCjFrtDD4j4umSzcbkn_custom_lang_ro" width="1" height="1" scrolling="no" frameBorder="0" style="display: none;"></iframe>' ).insertAfter( "footer" );
        }
    });
    $(document).on("click", ".get_reserve", function (e) {

        var my_form = $('#tab-pickup');

        var name = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var phone = my_form.find('.d_phone').val();
        var product_name = $('.title h1').text();
        var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
        var pickup = my_form.find('.htag > a.active').text();
        var price = '24 999';
        product_name = product_name.trim() + ' in magazinul: ' + pickup.trim();
        var web = 'https://darwin.md/apple-iphone-12-pro-max-128-gb-blue.html';

        if (name && phone && pickup) {
            $('.get_reserve').attr("disabled", true);
            $.ajax({
                url: '/' + lang + '/getDetailsA',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    name: name.trim(),
                    phone: phone.trim(),
                    product_name: product_name.trim(),
                    product_id: product_id.trim(),
                    price: price,
                    web: web,
                    canal: 'pickup'
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function (data) {
                    if (data.success == 'ok') {
                        thanks(data.message, 1);
                        $('.get_reserve').text(data.message);
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                        window.location.hash = '#success-pick_up';
                        dataLayer.push({'event': 'pickup_form'});
                        $( '<iframe src="https://creativecdn.com/tags?id=pr_9qCjFrtDD4j4umSzcbkn_orderstatus2_'+'24999'+'_'+data.order_id+'-pickup_ro-'+product_id.trim()+'&cd=default&id=pr_9qCjFrtDD4j4umSzcbkn_custom_lang_ro" width="1" height="1"scrolling="no" frameBorder="0" style="display: none;"></iframe>' ).insertAfter( "footer" );
                                                    //sendDataLayerSuccessProduct(data.order_id);
                                            } else {
                        thanks(data.message, 2);
                        thanksMobile(data.message , 2, $('#tab-pickup'));
                    }
                },
                error: function (resp) {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    if (resp.status == 406) {
                        var data = resp.responseJSON.data;
                        $('.get_reserve').attr("disabled", false);
                        for (var item in data){
                            $(my_form).find("input.d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                            thanks(data[item], 2);
                            thanksMobile(data[item] , 2, $('#tab-pickup'));
                        }
                        if(data === undefined || data.length == 0){
                            thanks(resp.responseJSON.message, 2);
                            thanksMobile(resp.responseJSON.message , 2, $('#tab-pickup'));
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } else {
            if (name == "" || name == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
                thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            if (phone == "" || phone == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
                thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            if (pickup == "" || pickup == undefined){
                thanks("Alege magazinul", 2);
            }
            thanksMobile(complete_all_input , 2, $('#tab-pickup'));
        }
        return true;
    });

    $(document).on("click", ".get_details", function (e) {

        var my_form = $('#more-info-form-modal');
        var valName = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var name = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var phone = my_form.find('.d_phone').val();
        var product_name = $('.title h1').text();
        var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
        var price = '24 999';
        var web = 'https://darwin.md/apple-iphone-12-pro-max-128-gb-blue.html';

        if (valName && phone) {
            $("button.get_details").attr("disabled", true);
            $.ajax({
                url: '/' + lang + '/getDetailsA',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    name: name.trim(),
                    phone: phone.trim(),
                    product_name: product_name.trim(),
                    product_id: product_id.trim(),
                    price: price,
                    web: web,
                    canal: 'info'
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function (data) {
                    if (data.success == 'ok') {
                        thanks(data.message, 1);
                        my_form.find('.modal-body').empty().html('<h2>' + data.message + '</h2>');
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                        window.location.hash = '#success-more_details';
                        dataLayer.push({'event': 'detalii_form'});
                                                    //sendDataLayerSuccessProduct(data.order_id);
                                            } else {
                        $(my_form).find("input").css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                        thanks(data.message, 2);
                        thanksMobile(data.message , 2, $('#more-info-form-modal'));
                    }
                },
                error: function (resp) {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    if (resp.status == 406) {
                        $("button.get_details").attr("disabled", false);
                        var data = resp.responseJSON.data;
                        $('.get_reserve').attr("disabled", false);
                        for (var item in data){
                            $(my_form).find("input.d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                            thanks(data[item], 2);
                            thanksMobile(data[item] , 2, $('#more-info-form-modal'));
                        }
                        if(data === undefined || data.length == 0){
                            thanks(resp.responseJSON.message, 2);
                            thanksMobile(resp.responseJSON.message , 2, $('#more-info-form-modal'));
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } else {

            if (valName == "" || valName == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            if (phone == "" || phone == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
            thanksMobile(complete_all_input , 2, $('#more-info-form-modal'));
        }
        return true;
    });

    $(document).on('click','.get_details, .get_preorder', function (e) {
    	sendDataLayerCheckoutArrayV4('view_cart');
    	sendDataLayerCheckoutArrayV4('personal_information');
        sendDataLayerCheckoutArray('view_cart', 1, 'view_cart');
        sendDataLayerCheckoutArray('personal_information', 2 ,'personal_information');
    });
    $(document).on('click','.get_credit', function (e) {

    $(document).on('click','.get_reserve', function (e) {
    	var option = ' ';
    	if($('#tab-pickup .htag a').hasClass('active')){
    		option = $('#tab-pickup .htag a.active').text();
    	}
    	sendDataLayerCheckoutArrayV4('view_cart');
    	sendDataLayerCheckoutArrayV4('personal_information');
    	sendDataLayerCheckoutArrayV4('shippimg_method');
        sendDataLayerCheckoutArray('view_cart', 1, 'view_cart');
        sendDataLayerCheckoutArray('personal_information', 2, 'personal_information');
        sendDataLayerCheckoutArray('shippimg_method', 4, option);
    });
    function sendDataLayerCheckoutArrayV4(d_event){
        var xobj=[];
        xobj= {
            'name': $('.tags').first().attr('data-prods'),
            'id': '81247',
            'price': '24999',
            'brand': $('.tags').first().attr('data-brand'),
            'category': $('.tags').first().attr('data-categ'),
            'variant': $('.tags').first().attr('data-prods').split(",").pop(),
            'quantity': 1
        };
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': d_event,
            'ecommerce': {
                'items':   xobj
            }
        });
    }
    function sendDataLayerCheckoutArray(d_event,d_step,d_option){
        var xobj=[];
        xobj= {
            'name': $('.tags').first().attr('data-prods'),
            'id': '81247',
            'price': '24999',
            'brand': $('.tags').first().attr('data-brand'),
            'category': $('.tags').first().attr('data-categ'),
            'variant': $('.tags').first().attr('data-prods').split(",").pop(),
            'quantity': 1
        };
        dataLayer.push({
        'event': 'gtmUaEvent',
            'gtmUaEventCategory': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
            'gtmUaEventAction': d_event,
            'gtmUaEventNonInteraction': 'True',
            'ecommerce': {
                'currencyCode': 'MDL',
                'checkout': {
                    'actionField': {'step': d_step, 'option': d_option},
                    'products':  xobj
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function sendDataLayerSuccessProduct(dorder_id){
        return true;
        //// sending from collect meansure protocol
        var revenue1 = '24999';
        var revenue = parseInt((revenue1*12.43)/100);
        var xobj=[];
        xobj= {
            'name': $('.tags').first().attr('data-prods'),
            'id': '81247',
            'price': '24999',
            'brand': $('.tags').first().attr('data-brand'),
            'category': $('.tags').first().attr('data-categ'),
            'variant': $('.tags').first().attr('data-prods').split(",").pop(),
            'quantity': 1
        };
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'gtmUaEvent',
            'gtmUaEventCategory': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
            'gtmUaEventAction': 'Purchase',
            'gtmUaEventNonInteraction': 'False',
            'ecommerce': {
                'currencyCode': 'MDL',
                'purchase': {
                    'actionField': {
                       'id': dorder_id,
                       'affiliation': 'Purchase',
                       'revenue': revenue,
                       'tax': '-',
                       'shipping': '-'
                    },
                    'products':   xobj
                }
            }
        });
        dataLayer.push({
            event: 'purchase',
            ecommerce: {
                currency: 'MDL',
                value: revenue,
                tax: '-',
                shipping: 0,
                affiliation: 'Purchase',
                transaction_id: dorder_id,
                items: xobj
            }
        });
    }
